    function toggle() {
      for (var i = 0; i < arguments.length; i++) {

        if (e) {

    function switchPastebinFriendly(link) {
      s1 = "Switch to copy-and-paste view";
      s2 = "Switch back to interactive view";
      link.textContent = link.textContent.trim() == s1 ? s2: s1;
      toggle('browserTraceback', 'pastebinTraceback');
      return false;
    }

        <li class="frame user">
          
            <code class="fname">/usr/local/lib/python3.12/site-packages/rest_framework/mixins.py</code>, line 68, in update
          

          
            <div class="context" id="c140303876269376">
              
                <ol start="61" class="pre-context" id="pre140303876269376">
                
                  <li onclick="toggle('pre140303876269376', 'post140303876269376')"><pre>    Update a model instance.</pre></li>
                
                  <li onclick="toggle('pre140303876269376', 'post140303876269376')"><pre>    &quot;&quot;&quot;</pre></li>
                
                  <li onclick="toggle('pre140303876269376', 'post140303876269376')"><pre>    def update(self, request, *args, **kwargs):</pre></li>
                
                  <li onclick="toggle('pre140303876269376', 'post140303876269376')"><pre>        partial = kwargs.pop(&#x27;partial&#x27;, False)</pre></li>
                
                  <li onclick="toggle('pre140303876269376', 'post140303876269376')"><pre>        instance = self.get_object()</pre></li>
                
                  <li onclick="toggle('pre140303876269376', 'post140303876269376')"><pre>        serializer = self.get_serializer(instance, data=request.data, partial=partial)</pre></li>
